## Text Elements
the function that has rate of change equal to f(x) ^75zzxdYe

it states that the signed area of a function is the antiderivative of that
function at the two extremis subtracted, because the derivative of that
function represent the instantaneous rate of change, equivalent to the square
metodology with infinite number of squares ^UqdMHTK8
